 The Gujjar Reservation Movement, which continued for 17 days in the state, came to an end on Wednesday after the agreement between the Rajasthan Cabinet sub-committee and Rajasthan Gurjar Reservation Struggle Committee
 rajasthan gurjar aarakshan sangharsh samiti ke adhyaksh karnal kirodi singh bansla or mantrimandal samiti ke adhyaksh grih mantri shanti dhariwal ne samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet ke dauraan yah ghoshnaa kii
 According to Colonel Bainsla, the government will conduct a survey of these castes in six months to give four percent reservation to the Special Backward Classes (gurjars, Gadiyaluhars, Banjaras and Rebari) in compliance with the order of the Rajasthan High Court
 in jatiyon ko maujuuda samay main mil rahaa ek pratishat aarakshan jari rahegaa
 Dhariwal said that the government will file a petition in the Rajasthan High Court urging the removal of the four percent reservation ban (on the lines of Karnataka and Tamil Nadu) till the reservation of special backward classes
 unhone kaha ki jatiyon ke survey karne ke uparant yadi vishesh pichhadaa varg main kuch anya jatiyaan judati hai, to anya pichhadaa varg (obisi) dwaara kii gai sifarish ke anusaar vishesh pichhadaa varg (esbisi) aarakshan alag se badha diya jayega
 Colonel Kirori Singh Bainsla held more than six hours of talks with the three ministers, Energy Minister Dr
 Jitendra Singh, Traffic Minister Brijkishore Sharma, under the chairmanship of Home Minister Shanti Dhariwal to resolve the reservation movement by the state government and to meet Chief Minister Ashok Gehlot
 Later, in front of reporters in the Government Secretariat announced to end the Gurjar agitation which was continuing for 17 days
 grahamantri dhariwal ne kaha ki gurjar andolanakaariyon par pichley or maujuuda andolan ke dauraan darj mukademon ko waapas lene par sahanubhutipurvak vichaar kiya jayega
 He said that apart from the four castes included in the Special Backward Classes, 82 castes will be surveyed

 In Aligarh and Jamia Millia Islamia University, a dispute has started between the government and the minority community regarding minority status
 chunaav or raajnneetik vajahon se ye maamla aane vaale samay main bad saktaa he
 Know what the Vice Chancellor of Jamia, Professor Talat Ahmed has to say on this matter and other controversies related to the university
 
 1
 aligarh or jamiya main alpsankhyak darje ko lekar vivaad shuru ho gaya he
 What is your stand? Answer: See, because this matter is still pending before the court, it would not be appropriate to say anything on it
 par haa, pehle bhi jamiya ko alpsankhyak darja sansad kii taraf se bane kamishan kii taraf se diya gaya
 Whatever is the matter in court, the decision will be made on the eyes
 jo log yahaan-vahaan meeting kar rahe hai is mudde ko lekar wo ye apane str par kar rahe hai
 2
 haal ke dinon main jamiya kai galat vajahon se khabaron main he
 For example, in response to many rtis, there have been errors in admissions and utilization of funds
 jawaab:main jab se yahaan aayaa hum chijen impruva kar rahaa hum
 i am trying to make it an academic university for the whole of India
 sirf upi, bihar yaa kashmir ke logon ke liye nahin
 We decided to take the engineering test with JEE so that the children from far flung areas would not have to come to Delhi for the test
 aise kadam uthaane par jo bekaar element the unako dikkat ho rahi he
 The wrong decisions taken during his time are being told through RTI
 artiai kaa galat istemaal ho rahaa he
 We are doing everything transparently
 3
 It is alleged that there were many wrongs in the school admission
 Answer: When i came across a first-generation learner, i got her admitted
 maan lo 50 kaa koi kota he or ek yaa do or bhi kar diya to koi bahut bada gunaah kar diya kya
 People do not know what to do and left from here
 4
 It is alleged that funds are being misused in the construction of VC office of the university
 Answer: No misuse is being done
 ye sirf visi offis nahin hoga, puraa complex hoga
 It will also have two big halls
 auditorium ke saath kai or bhi chijen hongi
 The old system is being completely rebuilt
 bijli par itnaa kharch hota tha jo ab kam hoga
 The entire building will be eco-friendly
 5
 Indian Prime Minister Narendra Modi emphasizes more on research and vocational training
 kya chal rahaa he is par uniwarsity main?jawaab:main ye proudli kah saktaa hum jamiya main GIAN ke tahat sabase zyada program chalaaye ja rahe hai
 The international ranking of the country's institutions is low
 iskaaryakramake jariye baahar ke research aayenge
 Knowledge will be shared
 long turm main bahut phayda hoga
 Most skill centers are opening in Jamia and under the Madan Mohan Malaviya scheme, the maximum support has been received from the government
 6
 You spoke to the government for help
 kya jamiya jaise alpsankhyak santhaan ko lekar sarkaraa kaa ravaiya barabari kaa he?jawaab:ye meraa ab tak kaa tajurba he ki issarkaar ne koi bhedbhaavamaare saath nahin kiya he
 We are getting all the funding from the government
 balkee dusron se zyada mil rahi he
 The difference is that earlier Jamia did not apply for all types of schemes, now it does
 hamaare do centre ko centre for excilence kaa certificate diya sarkaar ne
 There is nothing wrong in the intention of the government
 ye freedom mument se pehle kii uniwarsity he

 "this was said by Qazi Jahanara, Rajasthan's first lady in conversation with Saurabh Shukla of NDTV

 jahanara kaa janm gulabi shahar kahe jaanane vaale jaipur ke ramganj bazaar main akbar ali or shaukat aara ke ghar san 1971 main hua
 Jahanara's family was simple, and his father was a contractor in PWD and mother Begum Shaukat Ara was a housewife
 qaazi sahiba bataati hai ki contractor sahab kaa ramganj bazaar main rutaba tha, aakhir PWD main contractor the

 Its size is as big as the Earth

 yah goldilox kshetra main he, jahaan kaa taapmaana sahane laayak he, yani na to bahut garm or na hi bahut thanda
 This information was given by astronomer Geoff Marcy of the University of California, Berkeley
 unhone kaha ki ab tak paae gaye grahon main yah rahane yogya sabase behtareen grah he
 The results of this search are very reliable

 This telescope works on the change in light in space
